_maybe_reduce_max_tokens(oai_request: dict, error_msg: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"If the error is a context-length overflow, reduce max_tokens to fit. Sort and reset index to ensure consistent integer indexing\n        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n\n        all_signals = []\n        all_actuals = []\n\n        # Use expanding walk-forward\n        for train_df, valid_df, test_idx in self.validator.generate_folds(df_sorted):\n            if len(valid_df) < 10:\n                continue\n\n            X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n            y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n            X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n            y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n\n            # For this fold, get top N diverse models from population\n            top_models = population.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n\n            # Generate consensus signal using these models\n            consensus = ConsensusGate(\n                min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n                min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n            )\n\n            signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n\n            all_signals.append(signals)\n            all_actuals.append(y_valid)\n\n        if not all_signals:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0}\n\n        # Concatenate results\n        signal_series = pd.concat(all_signals)\n        actual_series = pd.concat(all_actuals)\n\n        # Get close prices using sorted df (indices align)\n        close_prices = df_sorted.loc[signal_series.index, \"close\"]\n\n        # Calculate metrics using simulator\n        self.trader.run(signal_series, close_prices)\n\n        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n\n        # Also compute raw directional accuracy\n        mask = (signal_series != -1) & actual_series.notna()\n        if mask.any():\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signal_series[mask] == actual_series[mask]).mean()\n        else:\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n\n        print(f\"Walk-forward results: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, Sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.4f}\")\n\n        return metrics\n\n    def train_best_models(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population,\n        horizon_data: dict = None\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Training best models on full data...\")\n\n        # Use recent data (last N days) for final training\n        recent_days = 60\n        cutoff_time = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=recent_days)\n        recent_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff_time].copy()\n\n        X_recent = recent_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_recent = recent_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Call train_best_models first.\")\n\n        signals = self.consensus_gate.decide(self.top_models, current_features)\n        return signals\n\n    def run_online_step(self, new_data: pd.DataFrame = None):\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute one iteration of the online evolution loop.\n\n        This is the main step method called repeatedly by Arbos.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n        print(\"RUNNING ONLINE STEP\")\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n        # 1. Prepare features\n        df = self.prepare_features(df)\n\n        # 3. Evolve population\n        population = self.evolve_population(X_train, y_train, generations=3)\n\n        # 5. Walk-forward validation on historical folds\n        metrics = self.run_walk_forward(df, population)\n\n        # 6. Train best models on full recent data and prepare horizon ensemble\n        self.train_best_models(df, population)\n\n        # 7. Save results\n        self._save_results(metrics, population, signals)\n\n        # Compile full result\n        result = {\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            \"accuracy\": metrics.get(\"accuracy\", 0.0),\n            \"bets_per_month\": metrics.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0),\n            \"sharpe\": metrics.get(\"sharpe\", 0.0),\n            \"max_drawdown\": metrics.get(\"max_drawdown\", 0.0),\n            \"total_return\": metrics.get(\"total_return\", 0.0),\n            \"latest_signal\": int(latest_signal) if latest_signal is not None else None,\n            \"population_fitness\": {str(i): ind.fitness for i, ind in enumerate(population.get_best(5))}\n        }\n\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n        print(\"STEP COMPLETE\")\n        print(f\"Metrics: {json.dumps(result, indent=2)}\")\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n        return result\n\n    def _save_results(self, metrics: dict, population: Population, signals: pd.Series):\n        \"\"\"Save results to disk.\"\"\"\n        timestamp = datetime.utcnow().strftime(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\")\n        run_dir = self.results_dir / timestamp\n        run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n        # Prepare features\n    print(\"Preparing features...\")\n    df = clean_data(df)\n    df = create_target(df, forward_periods=1)\n    horizon_features = generate_horizon_features(df, FeatureConfig.HORIZONS)\n    df = df.merge(horizon_features, on=\"open_time\", how=\"left\")\n    df = add_technical_indicators(df)\n    df = add_regime_features(df)\n    df = df.dropna(subset=[\"target\"]).ffill().dropna()\n    print(f\"Prepared {len(df)} samples with {len(df.columns)} columns\")\n\n    feature_names = [col for col in df.columns if col not in [\n        \"open_time\", \"open\", \"high\", \"low\", \"close\", \"volume\",\n        \"quote_volume\", \"trades_count\", \"future_close\", \"target\"\n    ]]\n    print(f\"Feature count: {len(feature_names)}\")\n\n    # Walk-forward split\n    validator = WalkForwardValidator(\n        train_days=ValidationConfig.TRAIN_DAYS,\n        valid_days=ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS,\n        step_days=ValidationConfig.STEP_DAYS,\n        min_train_samples=1000\n    )\n    trader = SimulatedTrader(\n        initial_capital=TradingConfig.INITIAL_CAPITAL,\n        fee_rate=TradingConfig.FEE_RATE,\n        slippage=TradingConfig.SLIPPAGE,\n        bet_size=TradingConfig.POSITION_SIZE\n    )\n\n    # We'll just do a single train/validation split for speed\n    cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=7)  # last week as test\n    train_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] <= cutoff].copy()\n    test_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] > cutoff].copy()\n\n    if len(train_df) < 1000:\n        print(\"ERROR: Not enough training data\")\n        return\n\n    X_train = train_df[feature_names]\n    y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n    X_test = test_df[feature_names] if len(test_df) > 0 else None\n    y_test = test_df[\"target\"] if len(test_df) > 0 else None\n\n    print(f\"Train: {len(X_train)} samples, Test: {len(X_test) if X_test is not None else 0}\")\n\n    # Initialize models\n    print(\"Initializing population...\")\n    pop = Population(\n        population_size=POP_SIZE,\n        model_types=MODEL_TYPES,\n        mutation_rate=0.3,\n        crossover_rate=0.4,\n        elitism_count=3\n    )\n    pop.initialize(input_dim=len(feature_names), feature_names=feature_names)\n\n    # Evolve\n    for gen in range(GENERATIONS):\n        print(f\" Generation {gen+1}/{GENERATIONS} starting\")\n        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n            try:\n                # Optional: scale data? For now raw\n                ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                if (i+1) % 2 == 0:\n                    print(f\"  Trained {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} individuals\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Error training {ind.model_type}: {e}\")\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n        pop.evolve()\n        best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n        print(f\"  Generation {gen+1} done. Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\")\n\n    # Evaluate on test\n    best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n    print(f\"\\nBest model: {best.model_type}\")\n\n    if X_test is not None and len(X_test) > 0:\n        try:\n            test_pred = best.model.predict(X_test, threshold=0.5)\n            test_accuracy = (test_pred == y_test).mean()\n            print(f\"Test accuracy: {test_accuracy:.4f}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Test error: {e}\")\n            test_accuracy = None\n\n    # Also try consensus with top 3\n    print(\"\\nConsensus evaluation:\")\n    top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=3)\n    consensus = ConsensusGate(min_models_agree=2, min_confidence=0.55)\n    signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_test)\n    mask = (signals != -1)\n    if mask.any():\n        consensus_accuracy = (signals[mask] == y_test[mask]).mean()\n        bet_count = mask.sum()\n        print(f\"  Consensus signals: {bet_count} bets\")\n        print(f\"  Consensus accuracy: {consensus_accuracy:.4f}\")\n    else:\n        print(\"  No signals generated\")\n        consensus_accuracy = 0\n        bet_count = 0\n\n    print(\"\\n=== MEDIUM TEST COMPLETE ===\")\n    result = {\n        \"best_fitness\": float(best.fitness),\n        \"test_accuracy\": float(test_accuracy) if test_accuracy is not None else None,\n        \"consensus_accuracy\": float(consensus_accuracy) if consensus_accuracy is not None else None,\n        \"bets\": int(bet_count),\n        \"train_samples\": len(X_train),\n        \"test_samples\": len(X_test) if X_test is not None else 0\n    }\n    print(f\"Result: {result}\")\n    return result\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Forward fill any remaining NaNs\n        df = df.ffill().dropna()\n\n        print(f\"Prepared {len(df)} samples with {len(df.columns)} columns\")\n        self.feature_names = [\n            col for col in df.columns\n            if col not in [\n                \"open_time\", \"open\", \"high\", \"low\", \"close\", \"volume\",\n                \"quote_volume\", \"trades_count\", \"future_close\", \"target\"\n            ]\n        ]\n\n        print(f\"Feature count: {len(self.feature_names)}\")\n        return df\n\n    def evolve_population(\n        self,\n        X_train: pd.DataFrame,\n        y_train: pd.Series,\n        generations: int = ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION\n    ) -> Population:\n        \"\"\"\n        Evolve a population of models.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(f\"Evolving population (input_dim={X_train.shape[1]})...\")\n\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(generations):\n            print(f\"  Generation {gen + 1}/{generations}\")\n\n            # Evaluate all individuals\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X_train)\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n\n                    # Simple fitness based on training accuracy (we'll validate on walk-forward later)\n                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n                except Exception as e:\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n            # Evolve\n            pop.evolve()\n\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n            print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\")\n\n        return pop\n\n    def run_walk_forward(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run walk-forward validation with the given population.\n        Uses multiple models to generate consensus signals and evaluate.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running walk-forward validation...\")\n\n        # pd.read_csv(self.data_path, parse_dates=[\"open_time\"])\n        else:\n            print(\"Fetching fresh data from Binance...\")\n            df = fetch_and_save_historical(\n                symbol=DataConfig.SYMBOL,\n                interval=DataConfig.INTERVAL,\n                start_date=DataConfig.START_DATE,\n                filepath=str(self.data_path)\n            )\n\n        if {df['open_time'].iloc[-1]}\", flush=True)\n        return df\n\n    def prepare_features(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        \"\"\"\n        Prepare feature matrix X and target y.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Preparing features...\", flush=True)\n\n        # Clean data\n        df = clean_data(df)\n\n        # Create target (next 15-minute direction)\n        df = create_target(df, forward_periods=1)\n\n        # Generate horizon ensemble features (these will be added as extra columns)\n        print(\"  Generating horizon features...\", flush=True)\n        horizon_features = generate_horizon_features(df, FeatureConfig.HORIZONS)\n\n        # Merge horizon features into df\n        df = df.merge(horizon_features, on=\"open_time\", how=\"left\")\n\n        # Drop rows with NaN in target\n        df = df.dropna(subset=[\"target\"])\n\n        # Forward fill any remaining NaNs\n        df = df.ffill().dropna()\n\n        print(f\"Prepared {len(df)} samples with {len(df.columns)} columns\", flush=True)\n        self.feature_names = [\n            col for col in df.columns\n            if col not in [\n                \"open_time\", \"open\", \"high\", \"low\", \"close\", \"volume\",\n                \"quote_volume\", \"trades_count\", \"future_close\", \"target\"\n            ]\n        ]\n\n        print(f\"Feature count: {len(self.feature_names)}\", flush=True)\n        return df\n\n    def evolve_population(\n        self,\n        X_train: pd.DataFrame,\n        y_train: pd.Series,\n        generations: int = ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION\n    ) -> Population:\n        \"\"\"\n        Evolve a population of models.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(f\"Evolving population (input_dim={X_train.shape[1]})...\", flush=True)\n\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(generations):\n            print(f\"  Generation {gen + 1}/{generations}\", flush=True)\n\n            # Evaluate all individuals\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X_train)\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n\n                    # Simple fitness based on training accuracy (we'll validate on walk-forward later)\n                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n                except Exception as e:\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n            # Evolve\n            pop.evolve()\n\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n            print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        return pop\n\n    def run_walk_forward(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run walk-forward validation with the given population.\n        Uses multiple models to generate consensus signals and evaluate.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running walk-forward validation...\")\n\n        # Sort and reset index to ensure consistent integer indexing\n        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n\n        all_signals = []\n        all_actuals = []\n\n        # Use expanding walk-forward\n        for train_df, valid_df, test_idx in self.validator.generate_folds(df_sorted):\n            if len(valid_df) < 10:\n                continue\n\n            X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n            y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n            X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n            y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n\n            # For this fold, get top N diverse models from population\n            top_models = population.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n\n            # Generate consensus signal using these models\n            consensus = ConsensusGate(\n                min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n                min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n            )\n\n            signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n\n            all_signals.append(signals)\n            all_actuals.append(y_valid)\n\n        if not all_signals:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0}\n\n        # Concatenate results\n        signal_series = pd.concat(all_signals)\n        actual_series = pd.concat(all_actuals)\n\n        # Get close prices using sorted df (indices align)\n        close_prices = df_sorted.loc[signal_series.index, \"close\"]\n\n        # Calculate metrics using simulator\n        self.trader.run(signal_series, close_prices)\n\n        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n\n        # Also compute raw directional accuracy\n        mask = (signal_series != -1) & actual_series.notna()\n        if mask.any():\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signal_series[mask] == actual_series[mask]).mean()\n        else:\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n\n        print(f\"Walk-forward results: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, Sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.4f}\")\n\n        return metrics\n\n    def train_best_models(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population,\n        horizon_data: dict = None\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Training best models on full data...\")\n\n        # Use recent data (last N days) for final training\n        recent_days = 60\n        cutoff_time = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=recent_days)\n        recent_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff_time].copy()\n\n        X_recent = recent_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_recent = Train horizon ensemble if not provided\n        if horizon_data is None:\n            print(\"Training horizon ensemble...\")\n            horizon_data = {}\n            for h_name, factor in FeatureConfig.HORIZONS.items():\n                if h_name == \"15m\":\n                    continue\n                # Resample and prepare features for this horizon\n                from .data.processor import resample_to_horizon\n                df_horizon = resample_to_horizon(recent_df, recent_days, factor)\n                if len(df_horizon) > 100:\n                    df_horizon = create_target(df_horizon, forward_periods=1)\n                    df_horizon = add_technical_indicators(df_horizon)\n                    df_horizon = add_regime_features(df_horizon)\n                    df_horizon = df_horizon.dropna()\n                    horizon_data[h_name] = df_horizon\n\n        self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n\n        self.main_population = population\n        self.top_models = top_models\n\n    def generate_current_signals(\n        self,\n        current_features: pd.DataFrame,\n        use_horizon: bool = True\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate trading signals for the most recent data points.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.top_models is None:\n            raise RuntimeError(\"Models not trained. Call train_best_models first.\")\n\n        signals = self.consensus_gate.decide(self.top_models, current_features)\n        return signals\n\n    def run_online_step(self, new_data: pd.DataFrame = None):\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute one iteration of the online evolution loop.\n\n        This is the main step method called repeatedly by Arbos.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n        print(\"RUNNING ONLINE STEP\", flush=True)\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n\n        # 1. Load/fetch latest data\n        if new_data is None:\n            df = self.load_or_fetch_data()\n        else:\n            df = new_data\n\n        # 2. Prepare features\n        df = self.prepare_features(df)\n\n        # 3. Split into recent data for training and current for prediction\n        # Use last 30 days for training, current for signal generation\n        recent_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=30)\n        train_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] <= recent_cutoff].copy()\n        current_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] > recent_cutoff].copy()\n\n        # Limit training samples to control memory/time (use most recent samples)\n        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES)\n            print(f\"Limited training to {len(train_df)} most recent samples\", flush=True)\n\n        if len(train_df) < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            print(f\"Insufficient training data: {len(train_df)} samples\")\n            return None\n\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # 4. Evolve population\n        population = self.evolve_population(X_train, y_train, generations=ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION)\n\n        # 5. Walk-forward validation on historical folds\n        metrics = self.run_walk_forward(df, population)\n\n        # 6. Train best models on full recent data and prepare horizon ensemble\n        self.train_best_models(df, population)\n\n        # 7. Generate current signals\n        if len(current_df) > 0:\n            current_features = current_df[self.feature_names]\n            signals = self.generate_current_signals(current_features)\n            print(f\"Generated {len(signals)} current signals\")\n            latest_signal = signals.iloc[-1] if len(signals) > 0 else None\n            print(f\"Latest signal: {latest_signal} (1=UP, 0=DOWN, -1=NO TRADE)\")\n        else:\n            signals = pd.Series()\n            latest_signal = None\n\n        # 8. Save results\n        self._save_results(metrics, population, signals)\n\n        # Compile full result\n        result = {\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            \"accuracy\": metrics.get(\"accuracy\", 0.0),\n            \"bets_per_month\": metrics.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0),\n            \"sharpe\": metrics.get(\"sharpe\", 0.0),\n            \"max_drawdown\": metrics.get(\"max_drawdown\", 0.0),\n            \"total_return\": metrics.get(\"total_return\", 0.0),\n            \"latest_signal\": int(latest_signal) if latest_signal is not None else None,\n            \"population_fitness\": {str(i): ind.fitness for i, ind in enumerate(population.get_best(5))}\n        }\n\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n        print(\"STEP COMPLETE\")\n        print(f\"Metrics: {json.dumps(result, indent=2)}\")\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n        return result\n\n    def _save_results(self, metrics: dict, population: Population, signals: pd.Series):\n        \"\"\"Save results to disk.\"\"\"\n        timestamp = datetime.utcnow().strftime(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\")\n        run_dir = self.results_dir / timestamp\n        run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n        # Save metrics\n        with open(run_dir / \"metrics.json\", \"w\") as f:\n            json.dump(metrics, f, indent=2)\n\n        # Save signals\n        signals.to_csv(run_dir / \"signals.csv\")\n\n        # Save top models\n        top_models = population.get_best(5)\n        model_dir = run_dir / \"models\"\n        model_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n            try:\n                ind.model.save(str(model_dir / f\"model_{i}_{ind.model_type}.pkl\"))\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"Could not save model {i}: {e}\")\n\n        #
